* Get elementor profile types.\n586\t\t */\n587\t\tpublic function wbcom_essential_elementor_profile_types() {\n588\t\n589\t\t\t$profile_types      = bp_get_member_types( array(), 'objects' );\n590\t\t\t$profile_types_data = array();\n591\t\t\tforeach ( $profile_types as $profile_type ) :\n592\t\t\t\tif ( ! empty( $profile_type->name ) ) {\n593\t\t\t\t\t$profile_types_data[ $profile_type->name ] = $profile_type->labels['singular_name'];\n594\t\t\t\t}\n595\t\t\tendforeach;\n596\t\n597\t\t\treturn $profile_types_data;\n598\t\n599\t\t}\n600\t\n601\t\t/**\n602\t\t * Render elementor member lists widget.\n603\t\t */\n604\t\tprotected function render() {\n605\t\t\t// Check if BuddyPress is active before rendering.\n606\t\t\tif ( ! function_exists( 'buddypress' ) ) * Get group types.\n565\t\t */\n566\t\tpublic function wbcom_essential_elementor_group_types() {\n567\t\n568\t\t\t$group_types      = bp_groups_get_group_types( array(), 'objects' );\n569\t\t\t$group_types_data = array();\n570\t\t\tforeach ( $group_types as $group_type ) :\n571\t\t\t\tif ( ! empty( $group_type->name ) ) {\n572\t\t\t\t\t$group_types_data[ $group_type->name ] = $group_type->labels['singular_name'];\n573\t\t\t\t}\n574\t\t\tendforeach;\n575\t\n576\t\t\treturn $group_types_data;\n577\t\n578\t\t}\n579\t\n580\t\t/**\n581\t\t * Render elementor group lists function render() {\n507\t\t\t// Check if bbPress is active before rendering.\n508\t\t\tif ( ! class_exists( 'bbPress' ) ) {\n509\t\t\t\tif ( current_user_can( 'manage_options' ) ) true : false;\n\n\t\t\t\t/* Loop through all the fields and check if fields completed or not. */\n\t\t\t\t$group_total_fields     = 0;\n\t\t\t\t$group_completed_fields = 0;\n\t\t\t\tforeach ( $single_group_details->fields as $group_single_field ) {\n\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t * If current group is repeater then only consider first set of fields.\n\t\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\t\tif ( $is_group_repeater ) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t\t * If field not a \"clone number 1\" then stop. array();\n\t\t$user_progress_formmatted = $this->get_user_profile_progress_formatted( $progress_details, $settings );\n\t\treturn $user_progress_formmatted;\n\t}\n\n\t/**\n\t * Get User profile get_user_profile_progress_formatted( $user_progress_arr, $settings ) {\n\n\t\t/* Groups */\n\n\t\t$loggedin_user_domain = bp_loggedin_user_domain();\n\t\t$profile_slug         = $profile_completion_percentage,\n\t\t\t);\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Group specific details\n\t\t */\n\t\t$listing_number = 1;\n\t\tforeach ( $user_progress_arr['groups'] as $group_id => $group_details user's profile completion %\n- Shows which profile fields/sections are complete\n- Circular or linear progress bar visualization\n- Only renders for logged-in users\n\n**Block 8: Member/Forums Activity**\n- ForumsActivity: Last forum discussion by logged-in user\n- Requires both BuddyPress AND bbPress\n- Shows topic title, reply count, last reply excerpt\n- Only renders for logged-in users with topics\n\n**Block 9: Forums List**\n- Displays recent forum topics\n- Shows topic avatar, title, author, reply count\n- Requires bbPress active\n- Sorting by date/popularity\n\n**Block 10: Dashboard Intro**\n- User greeting/welcome widget\n- Shows avatar, greeting text, user display name\n- Only renders for logged-in users\n\n**Block 11: Header Bar**\n- Complex navigation bar with user profile dropdown\n- Search icon, messages icon, notifications icon, cart icon\n- Feature flags: Dark mode (LearnDash), sidebar toggle (LearnDash)\n- WooCommerce integration for cart\n- BP version-aware URL functions\n- Multiple template files for dropdown sections\n\n---\n\n### COMMON PATTERNS ACROSS ALL BLOCKS:\n\n**BuddyPress Version Awareness:**\n- All group URL functions: `bp_group_url()` (12.0+) vs `bp_group_permalink()` (older)\n- User URL functions: `bp_members_get_user_url()` vs `bp_core_get_user_domain()`\n\n**Theme Detection:**\n- REIGN theme: custom layouts with cover images, online status indicators\n- BuddyX/BuddyxPro: simplified layouts\n- Generic Nouveau: standard BuddyPress layouts\n- Legacy theme: older template structure\n\n**Action Hooks Called:**\n- `bp_directory_members_actions` - friend requests, follow, message buttons\n- `bp_directory_groups_actions` - join/leave buttons\n- `bp_directory_members_item` - additional member data injection\n-
